+-
+-## Overview
+-
+-This document outlines the best practices, conventions, and standards used in the company backend application. The backend follows Domain-Driven Design (DDD) principles and implements a layered architecture to ensure code consistency, maintainability, and scalability. The stack is built on Java with Spring Boot, Spring Data JPA, and PostgreSQL.
+-
+-## Technology Stack
+-
+-### Core Technologies
+-- **Java 21**: Primary language using modern features (records, sealed classes, pattern matching)
+-- **Spring Boot 3.x**: Application framework with auto-configuration
+-- **Spring MVC**: RESTful web layer via `@RestController`
+-- **Spring Security**: Authentication and authorization (JWT / OAuth2)
+-- **Maven**: Build and dependency management
+-
+-### Database & ORM
+-- **PostgreSQL**: Relational database
+-- **Spring Data JPA + Hibernate**: ORM and repository abstraction
+-- **Flyway**: Database migration management
+-- **HikariCP**: Connection pooling (default in Spring Boot)
+-
+-### Testing Framework
+-- **JUnit 5**: Primary testing framework
+-- **Mockito**: Mocking framework for unit tests
+-- **Spring Boot Test (`@SpringBootTest`)**: Integration testing
+-- **MockMvc**: Controller/HTTP layer testing without a running server
+-- **Testcontainers**: Real database instances in integration tests
+-- **JaCoCo**: Code coverage — threshold: **90%** for branches, methods, lines, and instructions
+-
+-### Development Tools
+-- **Checkstyle / SpotBugs**: Code quality and static analysis
+-- **Lombok**: Reduce boilerplate (`@Getter`, `@Builder`, `@RequiredArgsConstructor`)
+-- **MapStruct**: Type-safe DTO ↔ entity mapping
+-- **SpringDoc OpenAPI (Swagger UI)**: API documentation
+-- **Docker Compose**: Local environment (PostgreSQL, etc.)
+-
+----
+-
+-## Architecture Overview
+-
+-### Domain-Driven Design (DDD)
+-
+-Domain-Driven Design is a methodology that focuses on modeling software according to business logic and domain knowledge.
+-
+-**Benefits:**
+-- **Improved Communication**: Promotes a common ubiquitous language between developers and domain experts.
+-- **Clear Domain Models**: Builds models that accurately reflect business rules and processes.
+-- **High Maintainability**: Dividing the system into bounded contexts and layers facilitates maintenance and evolution.
+-
+-### Layered Architecture
+-
+-```
+-┌─────────────────────────────────────┐
+-│        Presentation Layer           │  @RestController, @ControllerAdvice
+-├─────────────────────────────────────┤
+-│        Application Layer            │  @Service, @Transactional, DTOs
+-├─────────────────────────────────────┤
+-│          Domain Layer               │  Entities, Value Objects, Interfaces
+-├─────────────────────────────────────┤
+-│       Infrastructure Layer          │  JPA Repositories, Flyway, Config
+-└─────────────────────────────────────┘
+-```
+-
+-**Presentation Layer** (`src/main/java/.../presentation/`)
+-- Controllers handle HTTP requests and responses via `@RestController`
+-- Delegates all logic to Application layer services
+-- Uses DTOs (never exposes domain entities directly)
+-- Centralized exception handling with `@ControllerAdvice`
+-
+-**Application Layer** (`src/main/java/.../application/`)
+-- Services annotated with `@Service` and `@Transactional` orchestrate business logic
+-- Validates inputs via `@Valid` on DTOs with Bean Validation annotations
+-- Converts between DTOs and domain entities (via MapStruct mappers)
+-- Coordinates mucompanyple domain objects and repositories
+-
+-**Domain Layer** (`src/main/java/.../domain/`)
+-- JPA entities with business methods that enforce invariants
+-- Repository interfaces (Spring Data `JpaRepository` extensions)
+-- Domain exceptions that clearly communicate business rule violations
+-- Value Objects as `@Embeddable` classes or Java `record`s
+-- No Spring beans here — domain objects must be framework-agnostic where possible
+-
+-**Infrastructure Layer** (`src/main/java/.../infrastructure/`)
+-- Spring Data JPA repository implementations (auto-generated or custom `@Query`)
+-- Flyway migration scripts under `src/main/resources/db/migration/`
+-- External integrations (email, S3, etc.)
+-- Logging, configuration, and cross-cutting concerns
+-
+-### Project Structure
+-
+-```
+-backend/
+-├── src/
+-│   ├── main/
+-│   │   ├── java/com/company/
+-│   │   │   ├── domain/
+-│   │   │   │   ├── model/           # JPA entities & value objects
+-│   │   │   │   ├── repository/      # Repository interfaces
+-│   │   │   │   └── exception/       # Domain exceptions
+-│   │   │   ├── application/
+-│   │   │   │   ├── service/         # @Service classes
+-│   │   │   │   ├── dto/             # Request/Response DTOs
+-│   │   │   │   └── mapper/          # MapStruct mappers
+-│   │   │   ├── presentation/
+-│   │   │   │   ├── controller/      # @RestController classes
+-│   │   │   │   └── advice/          # @ControllerAdvice (GlobalExceptionHandler)
+-│   │   │   └── infrastructure/
+-│   │   │       ├── config/          # Spring config (@Configuration)
+-│   │   │       ├── logging/         # Logging utilities
+-│   │   │       └── security/        # Security config (JWT, filters)
+-│   │   └── resources/
+-│   │       ├── application.yml      # App configuration
+-│   │       └── db/migration/        # Flyway migrations (V1__init.sql, ...)
+-│   └── test/
+-│       ├── java/com/company/
+-│       │   ├── unit/                # Unit tests (Mockito, no Spring context)
+-│       │   └── integration/         # Integration tests (@SpringBootTest)
+-│       └── resources/
+-│           └── application-test.yml # Test configuration (H2 or Testcontainers)
+-├── pom.xml
+-└── docker-compose.yml
+-```
+-
+----
+-
+-## Domain-Driven Design Principles
+-
+-### Entities
+-
+-Entities are objects with a distinct identity that persists over time.
+-
+-**Before:**
+-```java
+-// Data handled as a plain Map or unstructured object with no behavior
+-Map<String, Object> candidate = new HashMap<>();
+-candidate.put("id", 1);
+-candidate.put("firstName", "John");
+-candidate.put("email", "john@example.com");
+-```
+-
+-**After:**
+-```java
+-@Entity
+-@Table(name = "candidates")
+-@Getter
+-@NoArgsConstructor(access = AccessLevel.PROTECTED) // JPA requires no-arg constructor
+-public class Candidate {
+-
+-    @Id
+-    @GeneratedValue(strategy = GenerationType.IDENTITY)
+-    private Long id;
+-
+-    @Column(nullable = false)
+-    private String firstName;
+-
+-    @Column(nullable = false)
+-    private String lastName;
+-
+-    @Column(nullable = false, unique = true)
+-    private String email;
+-
+-    @OneToMany(mappedBy = "candidate", cascade = CascadeType.ALL, orphanRemoval = true)
+-    private List<Education> educations = new ArrayList<>();
+-
+-    // Factory method — preferred over public constructor for complex creation
+-    public static Candidate create(String firstName, String lastName, String email) {
+-        Candidate c = new Candidate();
+-        c.firstName = Objects.requireNonNull(firstName, "firstName must not be null");
+-        c.lastName  = Objects.requireNonNull(lastName,  "lastName must not be null");
+-        c.setEmail(email); // delegate to setter that enforces invariant
+-        return c;
+-    }
+-
+-    // Domain method that enforces the business invariant
+-    public void setEmail(String email) {
+-        if (email == null || !email.contains("@")) {
+-            throw new IllegalArgumentException("Invalid email: " + email);
+-        }
+-        this.email = email;
+-    }
+-
+-    public void addEducation(Education education) {
+-        education.assignCandidate(this);
+-        this.educations.add(education);
+-    }
+-}
+-```
+-
+-**Explanation**: `Candidate` is an entity because it has a unique identifier (`id`) that distinguishes it from other candidates. Business rules (email validation) live inside the entity, not in the service or controller.
+-
+-**Best Practice**: Protect constructors with `AccessLevel.PROTECTED` for JPA and expose controlled creation via static factory methods. Enforce invariants inside domain methods.
+-
+----
+-
+-### Value Objects
+-
+-Value Objects describe aspects of the domain without conceptual identity. They are defined by their attributes, not by an identifier.
+-
+-**Before:**
+-```java
+-// Treating address as raw columns on the Candidate table
+-String street = "123 Main St";
+-String city = "Bogotá";
+-```
+-
+-**After:**
+-```java
+-@Embeddable // Stored as columns in the owning entity's table
+-public record Address(
+-    @Column(nullable = false) String street,
+-    @Column(nullable = false) String city,
+-    @Column(nullable = false) String country
+-) {
+-    // Compact constructor enforces invariants
+-    public Address {
+-        Objects.requireNonNull(street,  "street must not be null");
+-        Objects.requireNonNull(city,    "city must not be null");
+-        Objects.requireNonNull(country, "country must not be null");
+-    }
+-}
+-
+-// On the entity:
+-@Embedded
+-private Address address;
+-```
+-
+-**Explanation**: `Address` has no identity of its own — two addresses with the same fields are equal. Using Java `record` provides immutability and `equals`/`hashCode` automatically. `@Embeddable` maps it inline into the parent table.
+-
+-**Recommendation**: Prefer `record` for value objects to get immutability and structural equality for free. Only use `@Embeddable` classes when you need JPA mapping.
+-
+----
+-
+-### Aggregates
+-
+-Aggregates are clusters of objects treated as a unit, with a root entity that enforces consistency boundaries.
+-
+-**Before:**
+-```java
+-// Candidate and education managed separately, no boundary enforcement
+-Candidate candidate = candidateRepository.findById(1L).orElseThrow();
+-Education education = new Education();
+-education.setCandidateId(1L); // Bypasses the aggregate root
+-educationRepository.save(education);
+-```
+-
+-**After:**
+-```java
+-// All mutations to Education go through Candidate (aggregate root)
+-Candidate candidate = candidateRepository.findById(1L)
+-    .orElseThrow(() -> new CandidateNotFoundException(1L));
+-
+-Education education = Education.create("MIT", "Computer Science", LocalDate.of(2018, 1, 1));
+-candidate.addEducation(education); // Aggregate root manages its children
+-
+-candidateRepository.save(candidate); // Cascade saves Education automatically
+-```
+-
+-**Explanation**: `Candidate` is the aggregate root. `Education` and `WorkExperience` only exist in the context of a `Candidate`. All changes to these children must go through the aggregate root to maintain integrity.
+-
+-**Recommendation**: Use `CascadeType.ALL` and `orphanRemoval = true` on `@OneToMany` relationships within an aggregate so that child lifecycle is managed by the root via JPA cascading.
+-
+----
+-
+-### Repositories
+-
+-Repositories provide interfaces for accessing aggregates, encapsulating data access logic.
+-
+-**Before:**
+-```java
+-// Direct EntityManager usage scattered across service methods
+-@PersistenceContext
+-EntityManager em;
+-
+-public Candidate findById(Long id) {
+-    return em.find(Candidate.class, id);
+-}
+-```
+-
+-**After:**
+-```java
+-// Domain layer — defines the contract
+-public interface CandidateRepository extends JpaRepository<Candidate, Long> {
+-    Optional<Candidate> findByEmail(String email);
+-    boolean existsByEmail(String email);
+-
+-    // Complex queries use JPQL (type-safe) or native SQL only when justified
+-    @Query("SELECT c FROM Candidate c WHERE c.lastName = :lastName ORDER BY c.firstName")
+-    List<Candidate> findByLastName(@Param("lastName") String lastName);
+-}
+-```
+-
+-**Explanation**: Spring Data JPA generates the implementation automatically. Custom query methods follow Spring Data naming conventions or use `@Query` for complex cases.
+-
+-**Recommendation**:
+-- Prefer Spring Data method naming (`findBy`, `existsBy`, `countBy`) for simple queries.
+-- Use `@Query` with JPQL for complex filtering.
+-- Use native SQL (`nativeQuery = true`) only as a last resort; document the reason.
+-- Inject repositories via constructor injection in services.
+-
+----
+-
+-### Domain Services
+-
+-Domain Services contain business logic that doesn't naturally belong to any single entity or value object.
+-
+-**Before:**
+-```java
+-// Business logic scattered across utility methods with no clear home
+-public static int calculateExperienceYears(Candidate candidate) {
+-    // logic here
+-}
+-```
+-
+-**After:**
+-```java
+-@Service // Domain service — lives in the application layer, coordinates domain objects
+-@RequiredArgsConstructor
+-public class CandidateEvaluationService {
+-
+-    public int calculateTotalExperienceYears(Candidate candidate) {
+-        return candidate.getWorkExperiences().stream()
+-            .mapToInt(WorkExperience::getDurationInYears)
+-            .sum();
+-    }
+-
+-    public boolean isEligibleForSeniorPosition(Candidate candidate) {
+-        return calculateTotalExperienceYears(candidate) >= 5
+-            && candidate.getEducations().stream()
+-               .anyMatch(e -> e.getDegree() == Degree.BACHELOR || e.getDegree() == Degree.MASTER);
+-    }
+-}
+-```
+-
+-**Explanation**: Business logic that spans mucompanyple entities belongs in a dedicated service, not in controllers or repositories. This keeps domain rules testable and visible.
+-
+----
+-
+-### Additional Recommendations
+-
+-**Use of Factories**
+-
+-Implement static factory methods on entities or dedicated `XxxFactory` classes for complex creation logic.
+-
+-```java
+-public class InterviewFactory {
+-    public static Interview schedule(Candidate candidate, Position position, LocalDateTime at) {
+-        if (at.isBefore(LocalDateTime.now())) {
+-            throw new InvalidInterviewDateException("Interview must be scheduled in the future");
+-        }
+-        return Interview.create(candidate, position, at);
+-    }
+-}
+-```
+-
+-**Domain Events**
+-
+-Publish domain events using Spring's `ApplicationEventPublisher` to decouple side effects.
+-
+-```java
+-// In the entity or service:
+-eventPublisher.publishEvent(new CandidateCreatedEvent(candidate.getId()));
+-
+-// In a listener:
+-@Component
+-public class CandidateCreatedListener {
+-    @EventListener
+-    @Async
+-    public void onCandidateCreated(CandidateCreatedEvent event) {
+-        emailService.sendWelcomeEmail(event.candidateId());
+-    }
+-}
+-```
+-
+----
+-
+-## SOLID and DRY Principles
+-
+-### Single Responsibility Principle (SRP)
+-
+-Each class should have a single reason to change.
+-
+-**Before:**
+-```java
+-@RestController
+-public class CandidateController {
+-    @PostMapping("/candidates")
+-    public ResponseEntity<?> create(@RequestBody Map<String, Object> body) {
+-        // Validates input HERE
+-        if (body.get("email") == null) return ResponseEntity.badRequest().build();
+-        // Builds entity HERE
+-        Candidate c = new Candidate();
+-        c.setEmail((String) body.get("email"));
+-        // Persists HERE
+-        candidateRepository.save(c);
+-        return ResponseEntity.ok(c);
+-    }
+-}
+-```
+-
+-**After:**
+-```java
+-// Controller: only HTTP handling
+-@RestController @RequestMapping("/candidates") @RequiredArgsConstructor
+-public class CandidateController {
+-    private final CandidateService candidateService;
+-
+-    @PostMapping
+-    public ResponseEntity<CandidateResponse> create(@Valid @RequestBody CreateCandidateRequest request) {
+-        CandidateResponse response = candidateService.create(request);
+-        return ResponseEntity.status(HttpStatus.CREATED).body(response);
+-    }
+-}
+-
+-// Service: only business orchestration
+-@Service @Transactional @RequiredArgsConstructor
+-public class CandidateService {
+-    private final CandidateRepository candidateRepository;
+-    private final CandidateMapper candidateMapper;
+-
+-    public CandidateResponse create(CreateCandidateRequest request) {
+-        if (candidateRepository.existsByEmail(request.email())) {
+-            throw new DuplicateEmailException(request.email());
+-        }
+-        Candidate candidate = Candidate.create(request.firstName(), request.lastName(), request.email());
+-        return candidateMapper.toResponse(candidateRepository.save(candidate));
+-    }
+-}
+-```
+-
+----
+-
+-### Open/Closed Principle (OCP)
+-
+-Classes should be open for extension but closed for modification.
+-
+-**Before:**
+-```java
+-// Adding new notification type requires modifying this class
+-public class NotificationService {
+-    public void notify(String type, Candidate candidate) {
+-        if (type.equals("EMAIL")) { /* email logic */ }
+-        else if (type.equals("SMS")) { /* sms logic */ }
+-    }
+-}
+-```
+-
+-**After:**
+-```java
+-public interface CandidateNotifier {
+-    void notify(Candidate candidate);
+-}
+-
+-@Component
+-public class EmailNotifier implements CandidateNotifier {
+-    public void notify(Candidate candidate) { /* email logic */ }
+-}
+-
+-@Component
+-public class SmsNotifier implements CandidateNotifier {
+-    public void notify(Candidate candidate) { /* sms logic */ }
+-}
+-
+-// Adding a new channel = new class, no modification to existing code
+-@Component
+-public class PushNotifier implements CandidateNotifier {
+-    public void notify(Candidate candidate) { /* push logic */ }
+-}
+-```
+-
+----
+-
+-### Liskov Substitution Principle (LSP)
+-
+-Derived classes must be substitutable for their base class without altering program correctness.
+-
+-**Recommendation**: Prefer composition over inheritance. When inheritance is necessary, ensure that overriding methods honor the base contract (no throwing exceptions the base doesn't throw, no weakening postconditions).
+-
+-```java
+-// Good: interface-based composition
+-public interface CandidateStorage {
+-    Candidate save(Candidate candidate);
+-}
+-
+-@Repository
+-public class JpaCandidateStorage implements CandidateStorage {
+-    public Candidate save(Candidate candidate) { /* JPA */ }
+-}
+-
+-// Test double that fully satisfies the contract
+-public class InMemoryCandidateStorage implements CandidateStorage {
+-    private final Map<Long, Candidate> store = new HashMap<>();
+-    public Candidate save(Candidate candidate) { store.put(candidate.getId(), candidate); return candidate; }
+-}
+-```
+-
+----
+-
+-### Interface Segregation Principle (ISP)
+-
+-Many small, specific interfaces are better than one large general interface.
+-
+-**Before:**
+-```java
+-public interface CandidateOperations {
+-    Candidate findById(Long id);
+-    Candidate save(Candidate candidate);
+-    void sendWelcomeEmail(Candidate candidate);
+-    byte[] generateCvPdf(Candidate candidate);
+-}
+-```
+-
+-**After:**
+-```java
+-public interface CandidateRepository extends JpaRepository<Candidate, Long> { }
+-
+-public interface CandidateNotificationPort {
+-    void sendWelcomeEmail(Candidate candidate);
+-}
+-
+-public interface CandidateDocumentPort {
+-    byte[] generateCvPdf(Candidate candidate);
+-}
+-
+-// Services implement only the interface they actually need
+-@Service
+-public class CandidateService {
+-    private final CandidateRepository candidateRepository;
+-    private final CandidateNotificationPort notificationPort;
+-    // Does NOT depend on CandidateDocumentPort
+-}
+-```
+-
+----
+-
+-### Dependency Inversion Principle (DIP)
+-
+-High-level modules should depend on abstractions, not concrete implementations.
+-
+-**Before:**
+-```java
+-@Service
+-public class CandidateService {
+-    // Direct dependency on concrete JPA repository
+-    private final CandidateJpaRepository jpaRepo = new CandidateJpaRepository();
+-}
+-```
+-
+-**After:**
+-```java
+-@Service
+-@RequiredArgsConstructor // Constructor injection — preferred over @Autowired field injection
+-public class CandidateService {
+-    private final CandidateRepository candidateRepository; // Depends on interface
+-    private final CandidateNotificationPort notificationPort; // Depends on port interface
+-
+-    // Spring injects the concrete implementations at runtime
+-}
+-```
+-
+-**Rule**: Always use **constructor injection**. Never use `@Autowired` field injection — it hides dependencies and makes unit testing harder.
+-
+----
+-
+-### DRY (Don't Repeat Yourself)
+-
+-Reduce duplication by centralizing shared logic.
+-
+-**Before:**
+-```java
+-// Email validation duplicated in mucompanyple places
+-public void createCandidate(CreateCandidateRequest req) {
+-    if (!req.email().contains("@")) throw new IllegalArgumentException("Invalid email");
+-    // ...
+-}
+-public void updateCandidate(UpdateCandidateRequest req) {
+-    if (!req.email().contains("@")) throw new IllegalArgumentException("Invalid email");
+-    // ...
+-}
+-```
+-
+-**After:**
+-```java
+-// Centralized in the DTO with Bean Validation
+-public record CreateCandidateRequest(
+-    @NotBlank String firstName,
+-    @NotBlank String lastName,
+-    @Email @NotBlank String email  // @Email validates format once, everywhere
+-) {}
+-
+-// Or in a shared validator utility
+-public final class EmailValidator {
+-    private EmailValidator() {}
+-    public static void validate(String email) {
+-        if (email == null || !email.contains("@")) {
+-            throw new InvalidEmailException(email);
+-        }
+-    }
+-}
+-```
+-
+----
+-
+-## Coding Standards
+-
+-### Naming Conventions
+-
+-| Element | Convention | Example |
+-|---|---|---|
+-| Classes / Interfaces | PascalCase | `CandidateService`, `ICandidateRepository` |
+-| Methods / Variables | camelCase | `findById`, `candidateId` |
+-| Constants | UPPER_SNAKE_CASE | `MAX_CANDIDATES_PER_PAGE` |
+-| Packages | lowercase | `com.company.domain.model` |
+-| DB tables | snake_case | `work_experience` |
+-| DB columns | snake_case | `first_name`, `created_at` |
+-| Flyway migrations | `V{n}__{description}.sql` | `V2__add_resume_table.sql` |
+-
+-**All code, comments, logs, and error messages must be written in English.**
+-
+-```java
+-// Good
+-public Optional<Candidate> findByEmail(String email) {
+-    log.info("Finding candidate by email: {}", email);
+-    return candidateRepository.findByEmail(email);
+-}
+-
+-// Avoid
+-public Optional<Candidate> buscarPorCorreo(String correo) {
+-    log.info("Buscando candidato por correo: {}", correo);
+-    return candidateRepository.findByEmail(correo);
+-}
+-```
+-
+----
+-
+-### Java Usage
+-
+-- **Use Java 21 features**: records, sealed classes, pattern matching (`instanceof`), text blocks
+-- **Prefer `Optional<>`** over returning `null` from repository and service methods
+-- **Use `@NonNull` / `Objects.requireNonNull`** to document and enforce non-nullability
+-- **Avoid raw types**: always parameterize generics (`List<Candidate>`, not `List`)
+-- **Prefer immutability**: use `final` fields, records, and unmodifiable collections
+-
+-```java
+-// Good: explicit return type, Optional, no nulls
+-public Optional<Candidate> findById(Long id) {
+-    return candidateRepository.findById(id);
+-}
+-
+-// Avoid: returning null
+-public Candidate findById(Long id) {
+-    return candidateRepository.findById(id).orElse(null); // Don't do this
+-}
+-
+-// Good: use Optional.orElseThrow in the service
+-Candidate candidate = candidateRepository.findById(id)
+-    .orElseThrow(() -> new CandidateNotFoundException(id));
+-```
+-
+----
+-
+-### Error Handling
+-
+-Create domain-specific exception classes and handle them centrally.
+-
+-```java
+-// Domain exception
+-public class CandidateNotFoundException extends RuntimeException {
+-    public CandidateNotFoundException(Long id) {
+-        super("Candidate not found with id: " + id);
+-    }
+-}
+-
+-public class DuplicateEmailException extends RuntimeException {
+-    public DuplicateEmailException(String email) {
+-        super("A candidate with email already exists: " + email);
+-    }
+-}
+-
+-// Centralized HTTP mapping
+-@RestControllerAdvice
+-public class GlobalExceptionHandler {
+-
+-    @ExceptionHandler(CandidateNotFoundException.class)
+-    public ResponseEntity<ErrorResponse> handleNotFound(CandidateNotFoundException ex) {
+-        return ResponseEntity.status(HttpStatus.NOT_FOUND)
+-            .body(new ErrorResponse("NOT_FOUND", ex.getMessage()));
+-    }
+-
+-    @ExceptionHandler(DuplicateEmailException.class)
+-    public ResponseEntity<ErrorResponse> handleConflict(DuplicateEmailException ex) {
+-        return ResponseEntity.status(HttpStatus.CONFLICT)
+-            .body(new ErrorResponse("CONFLICT", ex.getMessage()));
+-    }
+-
+-    @ExceptionHandler(MethodArgumentNotValidException.class)
+-    public ResponseEntity<ErrorResponse> handleValidation(MethodArgumentNotValidException ex) {
+-        List<String> details = ex.getBindingResult().getFieldErrors().stream()
+-            .map(f -> f.getField() + ": " + f.getDefaultMessage())
+-            .toList();
+-        return ResponseEntity.badRequest()
+-            .body(new ErrorResponse("VALIDATION_ERROR", "Validation failed", details));
+-    }
+-
+-    @ExceptionHandler(Exception.class)
+-    public ResponseEntity<ErrorResponse> handleGeneric(Exception ex) {
+-        log.error("Unexpected error", ex);
+-        return ResponseEntity.status(HttpStatus.INTERNAL_SERVER_ERROR)
+-            .body(new ErrorResponse("INTERNAL_ERROR", "An unexpected error occurred"));
+-    }
+-}
+-```
+-
+-**Rule**: Never catch and swallow exceptions silently. Never let domain exceptions leak as HTTP 500.
+-
+----
+-
+-### Validation Patterns
+-
+-Use Bean Validation (`jakarta.validation`) on DTOs. Never validate in the controller body — let `@Valid` handle it.
+-
+-```java
+-// DTO with validation annotations
+-public record CreateCandidateRequest(
+-    @NotBlank(message = "First name is required")
+-    String firstName,
+-
+-    @NotBlank(message = "Last name is required")
+-    String lastName,
+-
+-    @Email(message = "Must be a valid email")
+-    @NotBlank(message = "Email is required")
+-    String email,
+-
+-    @Min(value = 0, message = "Years of experience cannot be negative")
+-    Integer yearsOfExperience
+-) {}
+-
+-// Controller — @Valid triggers validation before the method body executes
+-@PostMapping
+-public ResponseEntity<CandidateResponse> create(@Valid @RequestBody CreateCandidateRequest request) {
+-    return ResponseEntity.status(HttpStatus.CREATED).body(candidateService.create(request));
+-}
+-```
+-
+-For cross-field validation, use a custom `@Constraint` validator or validate inside the service before delegating to the domain.
+-
+----
+-
+-### Logging Standards
+-
+-Use SLF4J with Logback (default in Spring Boot). Always use parameterized logging.
+-
+-```java
+-@Slf4j // Lombok annotation generates a 'log' field
+-@Service
+-public class CandidateService {
+-
+-    public CandidateResponse create(CreateCandidateRequest request) {
+-        log.info("Creating candidate with email: {}", request.email());
+-        try {
+-            Candidate saved = candidateRepository.save(Candidate.create(...));
+-            log.info("Candidate created successfully with id: {}", saved.getId());
+-            return candidateMapper.toResponse(saved);
+-        } catch (DataIntegrityViolationException ex) {
+-            log.warn("Duplicate email attempt: {}", request.email());
+-            throw new DuplicateEmailException(request.email());
+-        }
+-    }
+-}
+-```
+-
+-**Log Level Guide:**
+-| Level | When to use |
+-|---|---|
+-| `ERROR` | Unexpected exceptions, system failures |
+-| `WARN` | Recoverable issues, constraint violations, deprecated usage |
+-| `INFO` | Significant business events (created, deleted, state change) |
+-| `DEBUG` | Detailed flow for development/troubleshooting |
+-| `TRACE` | Very verbose data (DB queries, payloads) |
+-
+-**Never log passwords, tokens, full credit card numbers, or PII.**
+-
+----
+-
+-## API Design Standards
+-
+-### REST Endpoints
+-
+-```
+-GET    /candidates           → List candidates (paginated)
+-GET    /candidates/{id}      → Get candidate by ID
+-POST   /candidates           → Create new candidate
+-PUT    /candidates/{id}      → Full update
+-PATCH  /candidates/{id}      → Partial update
+-DELETE /candidates/{id}      → Delete candidate
+-
+-GET    /candidates/{id}/applications  → Applications for a candidate
+-POST   /positions/{id}/interviews     → Schedule interview for position
+-```
+-
+-**Rules:**
+-- Use **nouns**, not verbs in paths (`/candidates`, not `/getCandidate`)
+-- Use **kebab-case** for mucompany-word path segments (`/work-experiences`)
+-- Use **plural** for collection resources
+-- Use **path variables** for identity (`/candidates/{id}`), **query params** for filtering (`?status=ACTIVE&page=0&size=20`)
+-
+----
+-
+-### Request/Response Patterns
+-
+-Use dedicated DTO records. Never expose JPA entities in the API response.
+-
+-```java
+-// Request DTO
+-public record CreateCandidateRequest(
+-    @NotBlank String firstName,
+-    @NotBlank String lastName,
+-    @Email @NotBlank String email
+-) {}
+-
+-// Response DTO
+-public record CandidateResponse(
+-    Long id,
+-    String firstName,
+-    String lastName,
+-    String email,
+-    LocalDateTime createdAt
+-) {}
+-
+-// Paginated list response
+-public record PageResponse<T>(
+-    List<T> content,
+-    int page,
+-    int size,
+-    long totalElements,
+-    int totalPages
+-) {}
+-```
+-
+-**Success response shape:**
+-```json
+-{
+-  "success": true,
+-  "data": { ... },
+-  "message": "Operation completed successfully"
+-}
+-```
+-
+----
+-
+-### Error Response Format
+-
+-```java
+-public record ErrorResponse(
+-    boolean success,
+-    String code,
+-    String message,
+-    List<String> details
+-) {
+-    public ErrorResponse(String code, String message) {
+-        this(false, code, message, List.of());
+-    }
+-    public ErrorResponse(String code, String message, List<String> details) {
+-        this(false, code, message, details);
+-    }
+-}
+-```
+-
+-```json
+-// 400 Bad Request
+-{
+-  "success": false,
+-  "code": "VALIDATION_ERROR",
+-  "message": "Validation failed",
+-  "details": ["email: Must be a valid email", "firstName: First name is required"]
+-}
+-
+-// 404 Not Found
+-{
+-  "success": false,
+-  "code": "NOT_FOUND",
+-  "message": "Candidate not found with id: 42",
+-  "details": []
+-}
+-```
+-
+----
+-
+-### CORS Configuration
+-
+-```java
+-@Configuration
+-public class CorsConfig {
+-    @Bean
+-    public CorsConfigurationSource corsConfigurationSource() {
+-        CorsConfiguration config = new CorsConfiguration();
+-        config.setAllowedOrigins(List.of(
+-            System.getenv().getOrDefault("FRONTEND_URL", "http://localhost:3000")
+-        ));
+-        config.setAllowedMethods(List.of("GET", "POST", "PUT", "PATCH", "DELETE", "OPTIONS"));
+-        config.setAllowedHeaders(List.of("*"));
+-        config.setAllowCredentials(true);
+-
+-        UrlBasedCorsConfigurationSource source = new UrlBasedCorsConfigurationSource();
+-        source.registerCorsConfiguration("/api/**", config);
+-        return source;
+-    }
+-}
+-```
+-
+----
+-
+-## Database Patterns
+-
+-### JPA / Hibernate Schema
+-
+-- **`@Entity` + `@Table`**: Always explicitly name tables in snake_case
+-- **`@Column`**: Always declare `nullable`, `unique`, and `length` constraints that mirror DB constraints
+-- **ID generation**: Use `GenerationType.IDENTITY` for PostgreSQL auto-increment
+-- **Auditing**: Use `@CreatedDate`, `@LastModifiedDate` via Spring Data `@EnableJpaAuditing`
+-- **Fetch strategy**: Always use `FetchType.LAZY` on `@OneToMany` and `@ManyToOne` unless there's a documented reason for `EAGER`
+-
+-```java
+-@Entity
+-@Table(name = "candidates")
+-@EntityListeners(AuditingEntityListener.class)
+-@Getter
+-@NoArgsConstructor(access = AccessLevel.PROTECTED)
+-public class Candidate {
+-
+-    @Id @GeneratedValue(strategy = GenerationType.IDENTITY)
+-    private Long id;
+-
+-    @Column(name = "first_name", nullable = false, length = 100)
+-    private String firstName;
+-
+-    @Column(name = "email", nullable = false, unique = true, length = 255)
+-    private String email;
+-
+-    @OneToMany(mappedBy = "candidate", cascade = CascadeType.ALL, orphanRemoval = true,
+-               fetch = FetchType.LAZY)
+-    private List<Education> educations = new ArrayList<>();
+-
+-    @CreatedDate
+-    @Column(name = "created_at", nullable = false, updatable = false)
+-    private LocalDateTime createdAt;
+-
+-    @LastModifiedDate
+-    @Column(name = "updated_at", nullable = false)
+-    private LocalDateTime updatedAt;
+-}
+-```
+-
+----
+-
+-### Migrations
+-
+-All schema changes **must** go through Flyway. Never use `spring.jpa.hibernate.ddl-auto=update` in production.
+-
+-```
+-src/main/resources/db/migration/
+-├── V1__create_candidates_table.sql
+-├── V2__create_positions_table.sql
+-├── V3__add_resume_column_to_candidates.sql
+-└── V4__create_interviews_table.sql
+-```
+-
+-**Migration naming**: `V{sequential_number}__{descriptive_snake_case_name}.sql`
+-
+-```sql
+--- V3__add_resume_column_to_candidates.sql
+-ALTER TABLE candidates ADD COLUMN resume_url VARCHAR(500);
+-CREATE INDEX idx_candidates_email ON candidates(email);
+-```
+-
+-**Rules:**
+-- Never modify an already-applied migration file — create a new one
+-- Include both the schema change and any required index creation in the same migration
+-- Test migrations on a local copy before committing
+-
+----
+-
+-### Repository Pattern
+-
+-```java
+-// Domain layer — interface only
+-public interface CandidateRepository extends JpaRepository<Candidate, Long> {
+-
+-    Optional<Candidate> findByEmail(String email);
+-    boolean existsByEmail(String email);
+-
+-    // Use JPQL for complex queries; keep it readable
+-    @Query("""
+-        SELECT c FROM Candidate c
+-        LEFT JOIN FETCH c.educations
+-        WHERE c.id = :id
+-        """)
+-    Optional<Candidate> findByIdWithEducations(@Param("id") Long id);
+-
+-    // Pagination support built-in
+-    Page<Candidate> findByLastName(String lastName, Pageable pageable);
+-}
+-```
+-
+-**Rules:**
+-- Inject via constructor (never `@Autowired` field injection)
+-- Return `Optional<>` for single-result queries — never return `null`
+-- Use `Page<>` and `Pageable` for list endpoints that might return large datasets
+-- Handle `DataIntegrityViolationException` in the service layer, not the repository
+-
+----
+-
+-## Testing Standards
+-
+-### Test File Structure
+-
+-- Test classes mirror the source structure: `CandidateService` → `CandidateServiceTest`
+-- Unit tests: no Spring context, pure Mockito — fast and isolated
+-- Integration tests: `@SpringBootTest` with Testcontainers or an H2 in-memory DB
+-- Maintain **90% coverage threshold** for branches, methods, lines, and instructions (enforced by JaCoCo)
+-
+----
+-
+-### Test Organization Pattern
+-
+-```java
+-// Unit test template
+-class CandidateServiceTest {
+-
+-    @Mock private CandidateRepository candidateRepository;
+-    @Mock private CandidateMapper candidateMapper;
+-    @InjectMocks private CandidateService candidateService;
+-
+-    @BeforeEach
+-    void setUp() {
+-        MockitoAnnotations.openMocks(this);
+-    }
+-
+-    @Nested
+-    @DisplayName("create()")
+-    class Create {
+-
+-        @Test
+-        @DisplayName("should create candidate when email is unique")
+-        void shouldCreateCandidate_whenEmailIsUnique() {
+-            // Arrange
+-            var request = new CreateCandidateRequest("John", "Doe", "john@example.com");
+-            var candidate = Candidate.create("John", "Doe", "john@example.com");
+-            var response = new CandidateResponse(1L, "John", "Doe", "john@example.com", null);
+-
+-            when(candidateRepository.existsByEmail(request.email())).thenReturn(false);
+-            when(candidateRepository.save(any(Candidate.class))).thenReturn(candidate);
+-            when(candidateMapper.toResponse(candidate)).thenReturn(response);
+-
+-            // Act
+-            CandidateResponse result = candidateService.create(request);
+-
+-            // Assert
+-            assertThat(result).isNotNull();
+-            assertThat(result.email()).isEqualTo("john@example.com");
+-            verify(candidateRepository).save(any(Candidate.class));
+-        }
+-
+-        @Test
+-        @DisplayName("should throw DuplicateEmailException when email already exists")
+-        void shouldThrowDuplicateEmailException_whenEmailAlreadyExists() {
+-            // Arrange
+-            var request = new CreateCandidateRequest("Jane", "Doe", "jane@example.com");
+-            when(candidateRepository.existsByEmail(request.email())).thenReturn(true);
+-
+-            // Act & Assert
+-            assertThatThrownBy(() -> candidateService.create(request))
+-                .isInstanceOf(DuplicateEmailException.class)
+-                .hasMessageContaining("jane@example.com");
+-
+-            verify(candidateRepository, never()).save(any());
+-        }
+-    }
+-}
+-```
+-
+----
+-
+-### Test Case Naming Convention
+-
+-- Use `@DisplayName` with clear behavior-driven descriptions: `"should [expected behavior] when [condition]"`
+-- Group related tests with `@Nested` inner classes labeled by the method under test
+-- Method names: `shouldDoSomething_whenCondition()` (camelCase)
+-
+----
+-
+-### Test Structure (AAA Pattern)
+-
+-Always follow the **Arrange → Act → Assert** pattern with clear section comments.
+-
+-```java
+-@Test
+-@DisplayName("should return candidate when found by ID")
+-void shouldReturnCandidate_whenFoundById() {
+-    // Arrange
+-    Long candidateId = 1L;
+-    Candidate mockCandidate = Candidate.create("John", "Doe", "john@example.com");
+-    when(candidateRepository.findById(candidateId)).thenReturn(Optional.of(mockCandidate));
+-
+-    // Act
+-    CandidateResponse result = candidateService.findById(candidateId);
+-
+-    // Assert
+-    assertThat(result).isNotNull();
+-    assertThat(result.email()).isEqualTo("john@example.com");
+-    verify(candidateRepository).findById(candidateId);
+-}
+-```
+-
+----
+-
+-### Mocking Standards
+-
+-- Use **Mockito** (`@Mock`, `@InjectMocks`, `when().thenReturn()`) for unit tests
+-- Use **`@MockBean`** only in `@SpringBootTest` integration tests
+-- Mock all external dependencies: repositories, external services, mappers
+-- Clear mocks in `@BeforeEach` (or rely on `MockitoExtension` which resets per test)
+-- Never use real database connections in unit tests
+-
+-```java
+-@ExtendWith(MockitoExtension.class) // Automatically resets mocks between tests
+-class CandidateServiceTest {
+-    @Mock private CandidateRepository candidateRepository;
+-    @InjectMocks private CandidateService candidateService;
+-}
+-```
+-
+----
+-
+-### Test Coverage Requirements
+-
+-Include these categories for each significant method:
+-
+-1. **Happy Path**: Valid input producing the expected result
+-2. **Error Handling**: Domain exceptions, database errors, not-found scenarios
+-3. **Edge Cases**: Empty lists, null values, boundary values
+-4. **Validation**: Bean Validation failures, business rule violations
+-5. **Integration Points**: Repository calls, mapper conversions, event publishing
+-
+-**Threshold**: 90% for branches, methods, lines, and instructions  
+-**Coverage Reports**: `mvn test jacoco:report` → `target/site/jacoco/index.html`  
+-**Coverage files**: Store dated reports as `YYYYMMDD-backend-coverage.md` in `coverage/`
+-
+----
+-
+-### Controller (MockMvc) Testing
+-
+-```java
+-@WebMvcTest(CandidateController.class)
+-class CandidateControllerTest {
+-
+-    @Autowired private MockMvc mockMvc;
+-    @Autowired private ObjectMapper objectMapper;
+-    @MockBean private CandidateService candidateService;
+-
+-    @Test
+-    @DisplayName("POST /candidates - should return 201 when valid request")
+-    void shouldReturn201_whenValidRequest() throws Exception {
+-        var request = new CreateCandidateRequest("John", "Doe", "john@example.com");
+-        var response = new CandidateResponse(1L, "John", "Doe", "john@example.com", null);
+-        when(candidateService.create(any())).thenReturn(response);
+-
+-        mockMvc.perform(post("/candidates")
+-                .contentType(MediaType.APPLICATION_JSON)
+-                .content(objectMapper.writeValueAsString(request)))
+-            .andExpect(status().isCreated())
+-            .andExpect(jsonPath("$.email").value("john@example.com"))
+-            .andExpect(jsonPath("$.id").value(1));
+-    }
+-
+-    @Test
+-    @DisplayName("POST /candidates - should return 400 when email is invalid")
+-    void shouldReturn400_whenEmailIsInvalid() throws Exception {
+-        var request = new CreateCandidateRequest("John", "Doe", "not-an-email");
+-
+-        mockMvc.perform(post("/candidates")
+-                .contentType(MediaType.APPLICATION_JSON)
+-                .content(objectMapper.writeValueAsString(request)))
+-            .andExpect(status().isBadRequest())
+-            .andExpect(jsonPath("$.code").value("VALIDATION_ERROR"));
+-    }
+-}
+-```
+-
+----
+-
+-## Performance Best Practices
+-
+-### Database Query Optimization
+-
+-- **Select only needed fields**: Use projections (DTO interfaces or records) instead of loading full entities when you only need a subset
+-- **Avoid N+1 queries**: Use `JOIN FETCH` in JPQL or `@EntityGraph` to load associations eagerly when needed
+-- **Pagination**: Always paginate list endpoints with `Pageable` — never return unbounded lists
+-- **Indexing**: Add `@Index` on `@Table` for frequently queried columns
+-
+-```java
+-// Avoid N+1: fetch association in a single query
+-@Query("SELECT c FROM Candidate c LEFT JOIN FETCH c.educations WHERE c.id = :id")
+-Optional<Candidate> findByIdWithEducations(@Param("id") Long id);
+-
+-// Projection for read-only list — avoids loading full entity
+-public interface CandidateSummary {
+-    Long getId();
+-    String getFirstName();
+-    String getEmail();
+-}
+-List<CandidateSummary> findAllProjectedBy();
+-```
+-
+----
+-
+-### Async Patterns
+-
+-Use `@Async` for fire-and-forget side effects (email, notifications). Never block on async operations in the request thread.
+-
+-```java
+-@Async
+-public CompletableFuture<Void> sendWelcomeEmail(String email) {
+-    // Non-blocking email dispatch
+-    return CompletableFuture.runAsync(() -> emailClient.send(email));
+-}
+-
+-// Parallel independent queries in a service
+-CompletableFuture<List<Candidate>> candidatesFuture = CompletableFuture.supplyAsync(
+-    candidateRepository::findAll);
+-CompletableFuture<List<Position>> positionsFuture = CompletableFuture.supplyAsync(
+-    positionRepository::findAll);
+-
+-CompletableFuture.allOf(candidatesFuture, positionsFuture).join();
+-```
+-
+----
+-
+-### Error Handling Performance
+-
+-- **Early return**: Validate and throw early to avoid unnecessary DB hits
+-- **Avoid over-wrapping**: Let exceptions propagate naturally to `@ControllerAdvice`
+-- **Don't use exceptions for flow control**: Use `Optional` or result types for expected "not found" scenarios
+-
+----
+-
+-## Security Best Practices
+-
+-### Input Validation
+-
+-- Validate all inputs at the DTO level via Bean Validation
+-- Sanitize string inputs to prevent SQL injection — rely on JPA parameterized queries (never string concatenation in `@Query`)
+-- Use `@PathVariable` and `@RequestParam` with type declarations — Spring rejects type mismatches automatically
+-
+----
+-
+-### Environment Variables
+-
+-Never commit secrets or credentials to version control.
+-
+-```yaml
+-# application.yml — uses environment variables with defaults for local dev
+-spring:
+-  datasource:
+-    url: ${DATABASE_URL:jdbc:postgresql://localhost:5432/company_db}
+-    username: ${DATABASE_USER:postgres}
+-    password: ${DATABASE_PASSWORD:postgres}
+-  jpa:
+-    hibernate:
+-      ddl-auto: validate   # NEVER 'update' or 'create' in production
+-```
+-
+-**Validate required variables at startup:**
+-
+-```java
+-@Configuration
+-public class EnvironmentValidationConfig {
+-    @Value("${DATABASE_URL}") private String databaseUrl; // Fails fast if missing
+-    @Value("${JWT_SECRET}")   private String jwtSecret;
+-}
+-```
+-
+----
+-
+-### Dependency Injection
+-
+-- **Always use constructor injection** — it makes dependencies explicit, final, and easy to test
+-- Never use `@Autowired` on fields
+-- Use `@RequiredArgsConstructor` (Lombok) to reduce boilerplate
+-
+-```java
+-// Good: constructor injection via Lombok
+-@Service
+-@RequiredArgsConstructor
+-public class CandidateService {
+-    private final CandidateRepository candidateRepository;  // final — immutable
+-    private final CandidateMapper candidateMapper;
+-}
+-
+-// Avoid: field injection
+-@Service
+-public class CandidateService {
+-    @Autowired private CandidateRepository candidateRepository; // Hidden dependency
+-}
+-```
+-
+----
+-
+-## Development Workflow
+-
+-### Git Workflow
+-
+-- **Feature branches**: Use descriptive names with a `-backend` suffix to work in parallel and avoid conflicts
+-  - e.g., `feature/jwt-authentication-backend`, `fix/duplicate-email-validation-backend`
+-- **Commit messages**: English, imperative mood, conventional commits format
+-  - `feat(candidate): add pagination to list endpoint`
+-  - `fix(auth): resolve JWT token expiry edge case`
+-  - `test(interview): add unit tests for scheduling service`
+-- **Small branches**: Keep branches small and focused on a single concern
+-- **Code Review**: All PRs must be reviewed before merging; reviewer checks architectural compliance
+-
+----
+-
+-### Development Scripts
+-
+-Run from the repository root (Gradle wrapper).
+-
+-```bash
+-# Run application locally
+-./gradlew bootRun
+-
+-# Run all tests
+-./gradlew test
+-
+-# Coverage report when JaCoCo plugin is configured (output: build/reports/jacoco/)
+-./gradlew test jacocoTestReport
+-
+-# Full verification when JaCoCo/quality gates are wired to `check`
+-./gradlew check
+-
+-# Build bootable JAR
+-./gradlew bootJar
+-
+-# Flyway via Gradle plugin (when configured)
+-./gradlew flywayMigrate
+-
+-# Docker Compose: start PostgreSQL locally
+-docker compose up -d postgres
+-
+-# Checkstyle (when plugin is configured)
+-./gradlew checkstyleMain checkstyleTest
+-```
+-
+-> **Legacy reference:** older docs may list `./mvnw` for the same intent (`spring-boot:run`, `test`, `verify`, Flyway Maven plugin); prefer the Gradle tasks above for this repository.
+-
+----
+-
+-### Code Quality
+-
+-- **Checkstyle**: Enforces naming, formatting, and import order. Run before every commit.
+-- **SpotBugs**: Static analysis for common bugs and security issues.
+-- **No compilation warnings**: Treat warnings as errors in CI (`-Werror` in Maven Enforcer).
+-- **All tests must pass** before merging — enforced in CI.
+-- **JaCoCo threshold**: Build fails if coverage drops below 90%.
+-
+----
+-
+-This document serves as the foundation for maintaining code quality and consistency across the company backend application. All team members should follow these practices to ensure a maintainable, scalable, and testable codebase.

++
++```bash

++```
++
++### Environment variables
++

++
++```env
++DATABASE_URL=postgresql+asyncpg://postgres:postgres@localhost:5432/openspec
++APP_NAME=open-spec-base-app
++APP_VERSION=0.1.0
++ENVIRONMENT=development
++```
++
++### Run database migrations
++
++```bash
++alembic upgrade head
++```
++
++### Run tests
++
++```bash
++pytest
++```
++
++### Lint and type check
++
++```bash
++ruff check .
++mypy src

++description: >
++  Frontend development standards for Angular projects.
++  Covers component architecture, state management, testing, and development workflow.

++
++# Angular — Standards and Best Practices
++
++## Technology Stack
++- Angular 17+ (standalone components)
++- TypeScript 5.x strict mode
++- NgRx or Angular Signals for state management
++- Angular Material or Tailwind CSS
++- Jest + Angular Testing Library (90% coverage threshold)
++- ESLint + Angular ESLint rules
++
++## Architecture
++```
++core/       Singleton services, guards, interceptors (providedIn: 'root')
++shared/     Reusable components, pipes, directives
++features/   One folder per domain area (components + containers + services + models)
++layout/     Shell, navigation, header components
++```
++
++## Key Rules
++- `ChangeDetectionStrategy.OnPush` on every component — no exceptions
++- Standalone components preferred over NgModules (Angular 17+)
++- Typed `FormGroup<T>` always — never untyped `FormGroup`
++- All API calls go through feature services — never directly inside components
++- Smart (container) components connect to state; dumb (presentational) components use `@Input`/`@Output` only
++- HTTP interceptor centralizes error mapping — services never catch HTTP errors individually
++
++## Naming Conventions
++| Element | Convention | Example |
++|---|---|---|
++| Components | PascalCase + suffix | `CandidateListComponent` |
++| Services | PascalCase + suffix | `CandidateService` |
++| Files | kebab-case | `candidate-list.component.ts` |
++
++## Testing
++- `TestBed` + Angular Testing Library
++- `HttpClientTestingModule` for service HTTP tests
++- 90% coverage enforced in `jest.config.ts`
++- AAA pattern; test name: `should do something when condition`
++
++## Git Workflow
++- Branch naming: `feature/<ticket-id>-frontend`
++- Commits: English, conventional commits

++# React + Vite — Standards and Best Practices

++- Zustand for client-only state

++- Vitest + React Testing Library (90% coverage threshold)

++## Architecture
++```
++api/         Typed API client functions (one file per resource)
++components/  Shared/reusable UI
++features/    Feature-scoped folders (components + hooks + types + index.ts)
++hooks/       Global custom hooks
++pages/       Route-level components

++- No business logic inside components — extract to custom hooks
++- Custom hooks wrap all API calls and expose `{ data, isLoading, error }`
++- React Query for all server state — no `useEffect` for data fetching
++- TypeScript strict: no `any`, explicit return types on all exported functions

++# Go + Gin — Standards and Best Practices
++

++- GORM + PostgreSQL

++- golangci-lint for static analysis
++
++## Architecture
++```
++internal/domain/         Pure Go structs + repository interfaces + error types
++internal/application/    Services + DTOs
++internal/presentation/   Gin handlers + middleware
++internal/infrastructure/ GORM repository impls + DB setup + Config
++```
++
++## Key Rules
++- All errors must be wrapped with context: `fmt.Errorf("service.Create: %w", err)`
++- Return `(T, error)` always — never panic in request handlers
++- Repository interfaces in domain; GORM implementations in infrastructure
++- golang-migrate for all schema changes — never use `AutoMigrate` in production
++- Constructor functions (`New<Type>`) enforce invariants
++- Gin `ShouldBindJSON` for input binding; centralized error middleware for responses
++
++## Naming Conventions

++| Files | snake_case | `candidate_service.go` |

++| Unexported | camelCase | `validateEmail` |
++| DB tables | snake_case | `work_experience` |
++| Migration files | `000001_description.up/down.sql` | `000002_add_resume.up.sql` |
++

++- `testing` package + testify for assertions
++- `httptest` for HTTP handler tests
++- Table-driven tests preferred for multiple cases
++- Test name: `TestCandidateService_Create_ShouldError_WhenEmailExists`
++- 90% coverage via `go test -coverprofile=coverage.out ./...`

++## Git Workflow
++- Branch naming: `feature/<ticket-id>-backend`
++- Commits: English, conventional commits

++description: >

++
++# Java Spring Boot — Standards and Best Practices
++
++## Technology Stack
++
++### Core
++- **Java 17**: records, sealed classes, pattern matching, text blocks
++- **Spring Boot 3.x**: auto-configuration, Spring MVC via `@RestController`
++- **Spring Security**: JWT / OAuth2
++- **Gradle**: build and dependency management (`./gradlew` always — never `mvn`)
++
++### Database & ORM
++- **PostgreSQL** as the relational database
++- **Spring Data JPA + Hibernate** for ORM and repository abstraction
++- **Flyway** for schema migrations (scripts at `src/main/resources/db/migration/`)
++- **HikariCP** for connection pooling
++
++### Testing
++- **JUnit 5** as the primary testing framework
++- **Mockito** for mocking in unit tests
++- **MockMvc** for controller/HTTP slice tests (no running server needed)
++- **Testcontainers** for real PostgreSQL in integration tests
++- **JaCoCo** for coverage enforcement — threshold: **90%** (branches, methods, lines, instructions)
++
++### Development Tools
++- **Lombok**: `@Getter`, `@Builder`, `@RequiredArgsConstructor`
++- **MapStruct**: type-safe DTO <-> entity mapping
++- **SpringDoc OpenAPI**: Swagger UI at `/swagger-ui.html`
++- **Checkstyle / SpotBugs**: static analysis
++
++---
++
++## Layered Architecture
++
++```
++Presentation   @RestController, @ControllerAdvice
++Application    @Service, @Transactional, DTOs, Mappers
++Domain         Entities, Value Objects, Repository interfaces, Exceptions
++Infrastructure JPA Repository impls, Flyway, Config, Security
++```
++
++### Rules per layer
++
++**Presentation**
++- Thin controllers — only HTTP handling, no business logic
++- Always use `ResponseEntity<>` with explicit status codes
++- Validate inputs with `@Valid @RequestBody` — never manually in method body
++- Never expose JPA entities; use DTOs
++
++**Application**
++- Annotate with `@Service` and `@Transactional`
++- Constructor injection always (`@RequiredArgsConstructor`) — never `@Autowired` on fields
++- Accept DTOs with `@Valid`; delegate to repositories and domain models
++- Catch `DataIntegrityViolationException` and rethrow as domain exceptions
++
++**Domain**
++- JPA entities with protected no-arg constructor and static factory methods
++- Business logic inside entity methods — not in services
++- Repository interfaces extend `JpaRepository<Entity, Long>`
++- Return `Optional<>` from repositories — never `null`
++
++**Infrastructure**
++- Spring Data JPA implementations (auto-generated or custom `@Query`)
++- Flyway scripts — naming: `V{n}__{descriptive_snake_case}.sql`
++- Never modify an already-applied migration
++
++---
++
++## JPA Entity Standards
++
++```java
++@Entity
++@Table(name = "candidates")
++@EntityListeners(AuditingEntityListener.class)
++@Getter
++@NoArgsConstructor(access = AccessLevel.PROTECTED)
++public class Candidate {
++
++    @Id @GeneratedValue(strategy = GenerationType.IDENTITY)
++    private Long id;
++
++    @Column(name = "first_name", nullable = false, length = 100)
++    private String firstName;
++
++    @Column(nullable = false, unique = true, length = 255)
++    private String email;
++
++    @OneToMany(mappedBy = "candidate", cascade = CascadeType.ALL,
++               orphanRemoval = true, fetch = FetchType.LAZY)
++    private List<Education> educations = new ArrayList<>();
++
++    @CreatedDate
++    @Column(name = "created_at", nullable = false, updatable = false)
++    private LocalDateTime createdAt;
++
++    @LastModifiedDate
++    @Column(name = "updated_at", nullable = false)
++    private LocalDateTime updatedAt;
++
++    public static Candidate create(String firstName, String email) {
++        Candidate c = new Candidate();
++        c.firstName = Objects.requireNonNull(firstName);
++        c.setEmail(email);
++        return c;
++    }
++
++    public void setEmail(String email) {
++        if (email == null || !email.contains("@"))
++            throw new IllegalArgumentException("Invalid email: " + email);
++        this.email = email;
++    }
++}
++```
++
++---
++
++## Naming Conventions
++
++| Element | Convention | Example |
++|---|---|---|
++| Classes / Interfaces | PascalCase | `CandidateService` |
++| Methods / Variables | camelCase | `findById`, `candidateId` |
++| Constants | UPPER_SNAKE_CASE | `MAX_CANDIDATES_PER_PAGE` |
++| Packages | lowercase | `com.company.domain.model` |
++| DB tables | snake_case | `work_experience` |
++| DB columns | snake_case | `first_name`, `created_at` |
++| Flyway scripts | `V{n}__description.sql` | `V2__add_resume_table.sql` |
++
++**All code, comments, logs, and error messages must be in English.**
++
++---
++
++## Error Handling
++
++```java
++// Domain exception
++public class CandidateNotFoundException extends RuntimeException {
++    public CandidateNotFoundException(Long id) {
++        super("Candidate not found with id: " + id);
++    }
++}
++
++// Centralized mapping
++@RestControllerAdvice
++public class GlobalExceptionHandler {
++
++    @ExceptionHandler(CandidateNotFoundException.class)
++    public ResponseEntity<ErrorResponse> handleNotFound(CandidateNotFoundException ex) {
++        return ResponseEntity.status(HttpStatus.NOT_FOUND)
++            .body(new ErrorResponse("NOT_FOUND", ex.getMessage()));
++    }
++
++    @ExceptionHandler(MethodArgumentNotValidException.class)
++    public ResponseEntity<ErrorResponse> handleValidation(MethodArgumentNotValidException ex) {
++        List<String> details = ex.getBindingResult().getFieldErrors().stream()
++            .map(f -> f.getField() + ": " + f.getDefaultMessage()).toList();
++        return ResponseEntity.badRequest()
++            .body(new ErrorResponse("VALIDATION_ERROR", "Validation failed", details));
++    }
++
++    @ExceptionHandler(Exception.class)
++    public ResponseEntity<ErrorResponse> handleGeneric(Exception ex) {
++        log.error("Unexpected error", ex);
++        return ResponseEntity.status(500)
++            .body(new ErrorResponse("INTERNAL_ERROR", "An unexpected error occurred"));
++    }
++}
++```
++
++---
++
++## Testing Standards
++
++```java
++@ExtendWith(MockitoExtension.class)
++class CandidateServiceTest {
++
++    @Mock private CandidateRepository candidateRepository;
++    @InjectMocks private CandidateService candidateService;
++
++    @Nested
++    @DisplayName("create()")
++    class Create {
++
++        @Test
++        @DisplayName("should create candidate when email is unique")
++        void shouldCreateCandidate_whenEmailIsUnique() {
++            // Arrange
++            var request = new CreateCandidateRequest("John", "john@example.com");
++            when(candidateRepository.existsByEmail(request.email())).thenReturn(false);
++            when(candidateRepository.save(any())).thenReturn(Candidate.create("John", "john@example.com"));
++
++            // Act
++            var result = candidateService.create(request);
++
++            // Assert
++            assertThat(result).isNotNull();
++            verify(candidateRepository).save(any(Candidate.class));
++        }
++
++        @Test
++        @DisplayName("should throw DuplicateEmailException when email already exists")
++        void shouldThrow_whenEmailAlreadyExists() {
++            var request = new CreateCandidateRequest("Jane", "jane@example.com");
++            when(candidateRepository.existsByEmail(request.email())).thenReturn(true);
++
++            assertThatThrownBy(() -> candidateService.create(request))
++                .isInstanceOf(DuplicateEmailException.class);
++            verify(candidateRepository, never()).save(any());
++        }
++    }
++}
++```
++
++**Coverage commands:**
++```bash
++# Run tests
++./gradlew test
++
++# Generate JaCoCo report (output: build/reports/jacoco/)
++./gradlew test jacocoTestReport
++
++# Verify threshold (fails build if below 90%)
++./gradlew check
++```
++
++---
++
++## REST API Standards
++
++- Nouns in paths (`/candidates`, not `/getCandidate`)
++- Kebab-case for multi-word segments (`/work-experiences`)
++- Plural for collections
++- Path variables for identity; query params for filtering and pagination
++
++```
++GET    /candidates           List (paginated)
++GET    /candidates/{id}      Get by ID
++POST   /candidates           Create
++PUT    /candidates/{id}      Full update
++PATCH  /candidates/{id}      Partial update
++DELETE /candidates/{id}      Delete
++```
++
++---
++
++## Security
++
++- Constructor injection always — never `@Autowired` on fields
++- Never commit secrets — use environment variables with `${VAR:default}` in `application.yml`
++- `spring.jpa.hibernate.ddl-auto=validate` in all environments — never `update` or `create`
++

++
++- Branch naming: `feature/<ticket-id>-backend`
++- Commits: English, imperative, conventional commits format
++- Small, focused branches — one concern per branch
++- All PRs require review before merging; CI must be green

++# Python + FastAPI — Standards and Best Practices
++
++## Technology Stack
++- Python 3.12+ — type hints mandatory on all functions and methods
++- FastAPI with Pydantic v2
++- SQLAlchemy 2.x (async) + PostgreSQL
++- Alembic for migrations (scripts under `alembic/versions/`)
++- pytest + httpx for testing (90% coverage threshold)
++- Ruff for linting + mypy (strict) for type checking
++
++## Architecture
++```
++domain/        Pure Python — no FastAPI or SQLAlchemy dependencies
++application/   Services + Pydantic DTOs + Mappers
++presentation/  FastAPI Routers + Depends() wiring + Exception handlers
++infrastructure/ SQLAlchemy repositories + DB session + Config
++```
++
++## Key Rules
++- Type hints required on every function signature — mypy strict enforced
++- Pydantic models validate all external input before reaching services
++- SQLAlchemy ORM models live only in `infrastructure/` — never imported in domain or application
++- Alembic for all schema changes — never use `Base.metadata.create_all()` in production
++- FastAPI `Depends()` for dependency injection — no manual service instantiation in handlers
++- Global exception handlers registered on the `app` instance for domain and validation errors
++
++## Naming Conventions
++| Element | Convention | Example |
++|---|---|---|
++| Files / Modules | snake_case | `candidate_service.py` |
++| Classes | PascalCase | `CandidateService` |
++| Functions / vars | snake_case | `create_candidate` |
++| DB tables | snake_case | `work_experience` |
++| Alembic scripts | auto-named | `abc123_add_resume_column.py` |
++
++## Testing
++- pytest with `pytest-asyncio` for async tests
++- httpx `AsyncClient` for HTTP integration tests
++- `pyproject.toml` enforces 90% coverage via `pytest --cov`
++- AAA pattern; test name: `test_should_do_something_when_condition`
++

++- Branch naming: `feature/<ticket-id>-backend`
++- Commits: English, conventional commits

++import asyncio
++import os
++import sys
++from logging.config import fileConfig
++
++from alembic import context
++from sqlalchemy import pool
++from sqlalchemy.engine import Connection
++from sqlalchemy.ext.asyncio import AsyncEngine, create_async_engine
++

++from src.infrastructure.config.settings import Settings  # noqa: E402
++from src.infrastructure.database.engine import Base  # noqa: E402

++config = context.config
++fileConfig(config.config_file_name)
++
++settings = Settings()
++config.set_main_option("sqlalchemy.url", settings.database_url)
++
++target_metadata = Base.metadata
++
++
++def run_migrations_offline() -> None:
++    url = config.get_main_option("sqlalchemy.url")
++    context.configure(url=url, target_metadata=target_metadata, literal_binds=True)
++
++    with context.begin_transaction():
++        context.run_migrations()
++
++
++def do_run_migrations(connection: Connection) -> None:
++    context.configure(connection=connection, target_metadata=target_metadata)
++
++    with context.begin_transaction():
++        context.run_migrations()
++
++
++async def run_migrations_online() -> None:
++    connectable = create_async_engine(
++        config.get_main_option("sqlalchemy.url"),
++        poolclass=pool.NullPool,
++        future=True,
++    )
++
++    async with connectable.connect() as connection:
++        await connection.run_sync(do_run_migrations)
++    await connectable.dispose()
++
++
++if context.is_offline_mode():
++    run_migrations_offline()
++else:
++    asyncio.run(run_migrations_online())

+ 
+-    - Common implementation steps:
+-        - Step 1: Create or update Flyway migration script (if schema change needed)
+-        - Step 2: Create or update JPA Entity in domain/model/ (@Entity, factory method, domain methods)
+-        - Step 3: Create or update Repository interface in domain/repository/ (extends JpaRepository)
+-        - Step 4: Create or update Request/Response DTOs in application/dto/ (with Bean Validation annotations)
+-        - Step 5: Create or update MapStruct Mapper in application/mapper/
+-        - Step 6: Create or update @Service class in application/service/ (with @Transactional)
+-        - Step 7: Create or update @RestController in presentation/controller/
+-        - Step 8: Register exception mapping in GlobalExceptionHandler (@ControllerAdvice) if new domain exceptions are introduced
+-        - Step 9: Write unit tests covering all layers (service, controller via MockMvc)
+-
+-    - Testing requirements:
+-        - Follow AAA pattern (Arrange / Act / Assert) in all tests
+-        - Unit tests use @ExtendWith(MockitoExtension.class) — no Spring context loaded
+-        - Controller tests use @WebMvcTest — mock the service layer with @MockBean
+-        - Integration tests use @SpringBootTest + Testcontainers (real PostgreSQL)
+-        - All existing unit tests must be reviewed and updated if affected by the change
+-        - All new unit tests must be green before merging
+-        - Full test suite must execute with 0 failures: ./gradlew test
+-        - JaCoCo coverage report (when configured): ./gradlew test jacocoTestReport
+-        - Coverage must meet 90% threshold: ./gradlew check (when JaCoCo verification is wired into check)
+-        - Database state must be properly restored after all integration tests (@Transactional on test class or manual cleanup)
+-        - All new endpoints must be manually tested with curl covering: happy path, validation errors (400), not found (404), conflict (409), server error (500)
+-        - All CREATE / UPDATE / DELETE curl tests must document the rollback or cleanup step
+-
+-    - Documentation requirements:
+-        - JPA entity / schema changes → Update ai-specs/specs/data-model.md (entity class + Flyway script)
+-        - API endpoint changes → Update ai-specs/specs/api-spec.yml
+-        - Standards / libraries / config changes → Update relevant *-standards.mdc files
+-        - All documentation must be written in English
+-
+-    - Error response format must follow this JSON structure:
+-        ```json
+-        {
+-        "success": false,
+-        "code": "ERROR_CODE",
+-        "message": "Human-readable description",
+-        "details": ["field: validation message"]
+-      }
+-        ```
+-        HTTP status code mapping:
+-          400 → VALIDATION_ERROR (Bean Validation failures, invalid input)
+-          404 → NOT_FOUND (entity not found by ID or key)
+-          409 → CONFLICT (unique constraint violation, duplicate email, etc.)
+-          422 → BUSINESS_RULE_VIOLATION (domain invariant broken)
+-          500 → INTERNAL_ERROR (unexpected exceptions)
+-
+-    - Implementation verification checklist must include:
+-        - Code Quality: no compilation warnings, Checkstyle passes, constructor injection used everywhere
+-        - Domain: entity has protected no-arg constructor + static factory method, business logic is in the entity not the service
+-        - Application: service is @Transactional, uses DTOs with @Valid, delegates to repository and domain — never to EntityManager directly
+-        - Presentation: controller is thin, uses ResponseEntity<>, all inputs validated with @Valid
+-        - Flyway: new migration script follows V{n}__description.sql naming, never modifies an existing applied script
+-        - Testing: all tests green, JaCoCo >= 90%, MockMvc tests cover all HTTP status codes
+-        - Integration: no N+1 queries introduced (use JOIN FETCH or @EntityGraph where needed)
+-        - Documentation: data-model.md, api-spec.yml, and relevant standards files updated

++from __future__ import annotations
++
++from uuid import UUID
++
++from src.application.dto.health_dto import HealthRequest, HealthResponse
++from src.domain.models.health import Health
++
++
++class HealthMapper:
++    @staticmethod
++    def to_domain(dto: HealthRequest, uptime_seconds: int, id: UUID | None = None) -> Health:
++        return Health.create(
++            id=id,
++            service_name=dto.service_name,
++            status=dto.status,
++            version=dto.version,
++            uptime_seconds=uptime_seconds,
++        )
++
++    @staticmethod
++    def to_response(health: Health) -> HealthResponse:
++        return HealthResponse(
++            id=health.id,
++            service_name=health.service_name,
++            status=health.status,
++            timestamp=health.timestamp,
++            version=health.version,

++from __future__ import annotations
++
++from datetime import datetime, timezone
++from uuid import UUID
++
++from src.application.dto.health_dto import HealthRequest, HealthResponse
++from src.application.mappers.health_mapper import HealthMapper
++from src.domain.exceptions.health_exceptions import HealthNotFoundError
++from src.domain.models.health import HealthStatus
++from src.domain.repositories.health_repository import HealthRepository
++
++
++class HealthService:
++    def __init__(self, repository: HealthRepository, app_start_time: datetime) -> None:
++        self._repository = repository
++        self._app_start_time = app_start_time
++
++    async def create(self, dto: HealthRequest) -> HealthResponse:
++        uptime_seconds = self._calculate_uptime_seconds()
++        health = HealthMapper.to_domain(dto, uptime_seconds)
++        saved_health = await self._repository.save(health)
++        return HealthMapper.to_response(saved_health)
++
++    async def get_by_id(self, id: UUID) -> HealthResponse:
++        health = await self._repository.find_by_id(id)
++        if health is None:
++            raise HealthNotFoundError(id)
++        return HealthMapper.to_response(health)
++
++    async def list_all(self) -> list[HealthResponse]:
++        health_records = await self._repository.list_all()
++        return [HealthMapper.to_response(record) for record in health_records]
++
++    async def update(self, id: UUID, dto: HealthRequest) -> HealthResponse:
++        existing = await self._repository.find_by_id(id)
++        if existing is None:
++            raise HealthNotFoundError(id)
++
++        uptime_seconds = self._calculate_uptime_seconds()
++        updated_health = existing.update(
++            service_name=dto.service_name,
++            status=dto.status,
++            version=dto.version,
++            uptime_seconds=uptime_seconds,
++        )
++        saved_health = await self._repository.save(updated_health)
++        return HealthMapper.to_response(saved_health)
++
++    async def delete(self, id: UUID) -> None:
++        existing = await self._repository.find_by_id(id)
++        if existing is None:
++            raise HealthNotFoundError(id)
++        await self._repository.delete_by_id(id)
++
++    def _calculate_uptime_seconds(self) -> int:
++        return int((datetime.now(timezone.utc) - self._app_start_time).total_seconds())

++from __future__ import annotations
++
++from http import HTTPStatus
++from uuid import UUID
++
++
++class HealthDomainException(Exception):
++    code = "HEALTH_DOMAIN_ERROR"
++    http_status = HTTPStatus.BAD_REQUEST
++
++    def __init__(self, message: str) -> None:
++        super().__init__(message)
++        self.message = message
++
++
++class InvalidHealthStatusError(HealthDomainException):
++    code = "INVALID_HEALTH_STATUS"
++    http_status = HTTPStatus.UNPROCESSABLE_ENTITY
++
++    def __init__(self, status: str) -> None:
++        super().__init__(f"Invalid health status: {status}")
++        self.status = status
++
++
++class InvalidHealthRecordError(HealthDomainException):
++    code = "INVALID_HEALTH_RECORD"
++    http_status = HTTPStatus.BAD_REQUEST
++
++    def __init__(self, field_name: str, value: object | None = None) -> None:
++        message = f"Invalid health record field: {field_name}"
++        if value is not None:
++            message = f"Invalid health record field: {field_name}, value={value}"
++        super().__init__(message)
++        self.field_name = field_name
++        self.value = value
++
++
++class HealthNotFoundError(HealthDomainException):
++    code = "HEALTH_NOT_FOUND"
++    http_status = HTTPStatus.NOT_FOUND
++
++    def __init__(self, health_id: UUID) -> None:
++        super().__init__(f"Health record not found for id: {health_id}")
++        self.health_id = health_id
++
++
++class DuplicateHealthRecordError(HealthDomainException):
++    code = "DUPLICATE_HEALTH_RECORD"
++    http_status = HTTPStatus.CONFLICT
++
++    def __init__(self, service_name: str) -> None:
++        super().__init__(f"Health record already exists for service: {service_name}")
++        self.service_name = service_name

++from __future__ import annotations
++
++from dataclasses import dataclass
++from datetime import datetime, timezone
++from enum import Enum
++from uuid import UUID, uuid4
++
++from src.domain.exceptions.health_exceptions import InvalidHealthRecordError, HealthNotFoundError
++
++
++class HealthStatus(str, Enum):
++    healthy = "healthy"
++    degraded = "degraded"
++    unhealthy = "unhealthy"
++
++
++@dataclass
++class Health:
++    id: UUID | None
++    service_name: str
++    status: HealthStatus
++    timestamp: datetime
++    version: str
++    uptime_seconds: int
++
++    @classmethod
++    def create(
++        cls,
++        service_name: str,
++        status: HealthStatus,
++        version: str,
++        uptime_seconds: int,
++        id: UUID | None = None,
++    ) -> "Health":
++        if not service_name or not service_name.strip():
++            raise InvalidHealthRecordError("service_name", service_name)
++
++        if not version or not version.strip():
++            raise InvalidHealthRecordError("version", version)
++
++        if uptime_seconds < 0:
++            raise InvalidHealthRecordError("uptime_seconds", uptime_seconds)
++
++        return cls(
++            id=id or uuid4(),
++            service_name=service_name.strip(),
++            status=status,
++            timestamp=datetime.now(timezone.utc),
++            version=version.strip(),
++            uptime_seconds=uptime_seconds,
++        )
++
++    def update(
++        self,
++        service_name: str,
++        status: HealthStatus,
++        version: str,
++        uptime_seconds: int,
++    ) -> "Health":
++        if not service_name or not service_name.strip():
++            raise InvalidHealthRecordError("service_name", service_name)
++
++        if not version or not version.strip():
++            raise InvalidHealthRecordError("version", version)
++
++        if uptime_seconds < 0:
++            raise InvalidHealthRecordError("uptime_seconds", uptime_seconds)
++
++        return Health(
++            id=self.id,
++            service_name=service_name.strip(),
++            status=status,
++            timestamp=datetime.now(timezone.utc),
++            version=version.strip(),
++            uptime_seconds=uptime_seconds,
++        )

++from __future__ import annotations
++
++from sqlalchemy import select
++from sqlalchemy.ext.asyncio import AsyncSession
++from uuid import UUID
++
++from src.domain.models.health import Health, HealthStatus
++from src.domain.repositories.health_repository import HealthRepository
++from src.infrastructure.database.models.health_orm import HealthORM
++
++
++class HealthRepositoryImpl(HealthRepository):
++    def __init__(self, session: AsyncSession) -> None:
++        self._session = session
++
++    async def find_by_id(self, id: UUID) -> Health | None:
++        orm = await self._session.get(HealthORM, id)
++        if orm is None:
++            return None
++        return self._to_domain(orm)
++
++    async def list_all(self) -> list[Health]:
++        result = await self._session.execute(select(HealthORM))
++        return [self._to_domain(row[0]) for row in result.fetchall()]
++
++    async def save(self, health: Health) -> Health:
++        existing = await self._session.get(HealthORM, health.id)
++        if existing is None:
++            orm = HealthORM(
++                id=health.id,
++                service_name=health.service_name,
++                status=health.status.value,
++                timestamp=health.timestamp,
++                version=health.version,
++                uptime_seconds=health.uptime_seconds,
++            )
++            self._session.add(orm)
++            await self._session.commit()
++            await self._session.refresh(orm)
++            return self._to_domain(orm)
++
++        existing.service_name = health.service_name
++        existing.status = health.status.value
++        existing.timestamp = health.timestamp
++        existing.version = health.version
++        existing.uptime_seconds = health.uptime_seconds
++        await self._session.commit()
++        await self._session.refresh(existing)
++        return self._to_domain(existing)
++
++    async def delete_by_id(self, id: UUID) -> None:
++        orm = await self._session.get(HealthORM, id)
++        if orm is None:
++            return
++        await self._session.delete(orm)
++        await self._session.commit()
++
++    @staticmethod
++    def _to_domain(orm: HealthORM) -> Health:
++        return Health(
++            id=orm.id,
++            service_name=orm.service_name,
++            status=HealthStatus(orm.status),
++            timestamp=orm.timestamp,
++            version=orm.version,
++            uptime_seconds=orm.uptime_seconds,
++        )

++from __future__ import annotations
++
++from fastapi import FastAPI, HTTPException, Request
++from fastapi.exceptions import RequestValidationError
++from fastapi.responses import JSONResponse
++
++from src.domain.exceptions.health_exceptions import HealthDomainException
++
++
++def register_exception_handlers(app: FastAPI) -> None:
++    @app.exception_handler(HealthDomainException)
++    async def health_domain_exception_handler(request: Request, exc: HealthDomainException) -> JSONResponse:
++        return JSONResponse(
++            status_code=exc.http_status,
++            content={
++                "success": False,
++                "code": exc.code,
++                "message": exc.message,
++                "details": [],
++            },
++        )
++
++    @app.exception_handler(RequestValidationError)
++    async def validation_exception_handler(request: Request, exc: RequestValidationError) -> JSONResponse:
++        return JSONResponse(
++            status_code=422,
++            content={
++                "success": False,
++                "code": "VALIDATION_ERROR",
++                "message": "Validation failed",
++                "details": exc.errors(),
++            },
++        )
++
++    @app.exception_handler(HTTPException)
++    async def http_exception_handler(request: Request, exc: HTTPException) -> JSONResponse:
++        return JSONResponse(
++            status_code=exc.status_code,
++            content={
++                "success": False,
++                "code": "HTTP_EXCEPTION",
++                "message": exc.detail,
++                "details": [],
++            },
++        )

++        "version": "1.0.0",
++    }
++
